< review>
It's a pretty decent little cineplex with great digital projectors. The prices are good, the concessions almost reasonable, but the parking blows. The  theatre itself has a tiny little lot off the to left, but once it's fill, it's every man, woman and child for themselves. On most nights downtown Fairfax is pretty packed, and with limited parking for the entire downtown area, it only compounds the problem. It's not a reason to avoid the place by any means, just more of a cautionary tale. Expect to do some walking.< /review>

When I walked in i spotted the 2 boxes tagged with my name on it. I proceeded to the back to ask for 1 more additional shoe and a couple other items. There were at LEAST 5 maybe 6 store associates working and only 2 other customers but the service was sooooo SLOW. I finally got the additional pair which was damaged about 15 mins later! I then asked for them to switch them out another pair and pointed out the damage, the associate said he would and then sent a different associate out 10 mins later with what I assumed was the fresh pair, luckily i looked in the box because it was the same EXACT pair w the defect after the associate had just confirmed he switched them for another pair. I then get to the register, (15 mins later) and the 2 boxes are gone! Oddly enough the teen in front if me just so happens to be buying a pair of the EXACT same color and size i had on hold that have now went missing. Another 10 mins go by and the Manager comes from the back (From looking for my order that they KNOW theyre selling to the kid in front of me) saying they cant find my shoes. Almost ruined my daughters Van's themed Birthday.
